<tr><td width="742"><h3><a href="https://github.com/1992513/djy/blob/master/gb/26/1/19/n14679684.md#1" target="_blank">澳国庆长周末各州商家与服务情况一览</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/1992513/djy/blob/master/gb/26/1/19/n14679684.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2021/01/4302b340178a4ee8671e4ba1b9f7a12b-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>下周一（1月26日）是澳洲国庆日，澳洲人将迎来三天假期，许多民众会放松身心，或计划烧烤，或与朋友聚会，或外出购物及参加各式庆祝活动。
